/* ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   SCROLL REVEAL
   CSS side only — opacity + transform.
   Add a Custom Code block with the JS below (see comment).
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
.mbs3-reveal {
  opacity:    0;
  transform:  translateY(22px);
  transition: opacity .55s ease, transform .55s ease;
}
.mbs3-reveal.is-visible {
  opacity:   1;
  transform: none;
}
.mbs3-reveal-d1 { transition-delay: .10s; }
.mbs3-reveal-d2 { transition-delay: .20s; }
.mbs3-reveal-d3 { transition-delay: .30s; }

/*
   ── SCROLL REVEAL JS (paste into a Custom Code block) ──

   <script>
   (function(){
     var els = document.querySelectorAll('.mbs3-reveal');
     if(!els.length) return;
     var io = new IntersectionObserver(function(entries, obs){
       entries.forEach(function(e){
         if(e.isIntersecting){ e.target.classList.add('is-visible'); obs.unobserve(e.target); }
       });
     }, { threshold: 0.12 });
     els.forEach(function(el){ io.observe(el); });
   })();
   </script>

   Then add class "mbs3-reveal" (+ optionally mbs3-reveal-d1/d2/d3)
   to any card, heading, or stat block you want to animate in.
*/

/* ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   SCROLL REVEAL
   CSS side only — opacity + transform.
   Add a Custom Code block with the JS below (see comment).
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
.mbs3-reveal {
  opacity:    0;
  transform:  translateY(22px);
  transition: opacity .55s ease, transform .55s ease;

  opacity:   1;
  transform: none;
}

.mbs3-reveal-d2 { transition-delay: .20s; }

/*
   ── SCROLL REVEAL JS (paste into a Custom Code block) ──

   <script>
   (function(){
     var els = document.querySelectorAll('.mbs3-reveal');
     if(!els.length) return;
     var io = new IntersectionObserver(function(entries, obs){
       entries.forEach(function(e){
         if(e.isIntersecting){ e.target.classList.add('is-visible'); obs.unobserve(e.target); }
       });
     }, { threshold: 0.12 });
     els.forEach(function(el){ io.observe(el); });
   })();
   </script>

   Then add class "mbs3-reveal" (+ optionally mbs3-reveal-d1/d2/d3)
   to any card, heading, or stat block you want to animate in.
*/
